   <script>
    window.lazyloadingConfig = {
         networkSpeedFactor: function(speedChangeCallback) {
             var initialSpeed = 1.0;
             
             var connection = navigator.connection || navigator.mozConnection || navigator.webkitConnection;
 
             function onConnectionChange() {
                 if(speedChangeCallback) {
                     speedChangeCallback(getSpeed());
                 }
             }
 
             function getSpeed() {
                 var retVal = 1;
 
                 if(!connection.effectiveType) {
                     return retVal;
                 }
 
                 switch(connection.effectiveType) {
                     case '4g':
                         retVal = 1;
                         break;
                     case '3g':
                         retVal = 0.5;
                         break;
                     default:
                         retVal = 0.2;
                         break;
                 }
 
                 return retVal;
             }
 
             function bindChangeListeners() {
                 connection.addEventListener('typechange', onConnectionChange);
             }
 
 
             if(connection) {
                 bindChangeListeners();
                 return initialSpeed === 1 ? getSpeed() : initialSpeed;
             } else {
                 return initialSpeed;
             }
 
 
         }
     }
   </script>

      <div class="block ">
       <div class="embedded" data-html-asset-id="163806">
        <a class="html-is-seuraa html-is-seuraa-myynti" href="https://tilaa.sanoma.fi/hs-digi-jatka?aid=Z9NMJZ45VM&amp;ref=nayte_jatko" id="tikkeri" style="display:none; text-align: left;">
         <h3>
          Käytössäsi on kahden viikon tutustumistilaus.
          <span class="label">
           Jatka tästä
          </span>
          kuukausi maksutta.
         </h3>
        </a>
        <script>
         (function () {
     var productSortOrder = [ "HSVERKKOPLUS", "HSVERKKO" ];
 
     window.showElementsBasedOnEntitlements = function () {
         try {
             var parsedProfile = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('IS-userprofile'));
             var filteredEntitlements = parsedProfile.fullEntitlements.filter(function(entitlement) {
                 return productSortOrder.indexOf(entitlement.productId) !== -1;
             });
             sortedEntitlements = filteredEntitlements.sort(function (item1, item2) {                               
                 var samplesubs = 'samplesubs';
                 var item1Sample = getEntitlementAttributeValue(item1, samplesubs) === '1';
                 var item2Sample = getEntitlementAttributeValue(item2, samplesubs) === '1';
                 if (item1Sample && !item2Sample) {
                     return -1;
                 } else if (!item1Sample && item2Sample) {
                     return 1;
                 }
                 var prodIdDiff = productSortOrder.indexOf(item1.productId) - productSortOrder.indexOf(item2.productId);
                 if (prodIdDiff != 0) {
                     return prodIdDiff;
                 }
                 return new Date(item2.endDate) - new Date(item1.endDate);
             })
             
             if (sortedEntitlements.length > 0) {
                 showEntitlementBasedElements(sortedEntitlements);
             }
         } catch (error) { }
     }
 
     function showEntitlementBasedElements(sortedEntitlements) {
         showWhenSample(sortedEntitlements, "#tikkeri");
     }
 
     function showWhenSample(sortedEntitlements, selector) {
         if (getEntitlementAttributeValue(sortedEntitlements[0], "samplesubs") === "1") {
             showElement(selector);
         }
     }
 
     function getEntitlementAttributeValue(entitlement, attributeKey) {
         var attributes = entitlement.entitlementAttributes.filter(function (att) {
             return att.key === attributeKey;
         });
 
         if (attributes.length > 0 && attributes[0].value !== undefined) {
             return attributes[0].value;
         }
         return undefined;
     }
 
     function showElement(selector) {
         $(selector).css("display", "block");
     }
 })();
        </script>
        <script>
         window.showElementsBasedOnEntitlements();
         window.Events.bind('subscription', function(e, subscription) {
             window.showElementsBasedOnEntitlements();
         });
        </script>

    (function() {
         // Load detector on a sample of page loads
         // Ratio should be a number between 0 and 1
         //     - 0 means 'never load'
         //     - 0.333 means 'load on every three page loads'
         //     - 1 means 'always load'
         var sabdetect_sample_ratio = 10/100;
 
         window.Sabdetect_load = Math.random() < sabdetect_sample_ratio;
 
         if (window.Sabdetect_load) {
             var sabd = document.createElement('script');
             sabd.type = 'text/javascript';
             sabd.async = true;
             sabd.src = '//sn.sanoma.fi/js/sabdetect/Sabdetect-is-async.min.js';
             var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
             s.parentNode.insertBefore(sabd, s);
         }
     })();
   </script>
